<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> We currently plan to 
complete our 12 Eagle Ford well inventory in the third and fourth quarters of 
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;These wells are in four units located in Karnes County, Texas 
(33% operated working interest) and Fayette County, Texas (50% working 
interest), two of which are held by production and the other two are in the
primary term of leases.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">In addition, pending 
commodity prices, we plan to drill five to six gross Eagle Ford wells (33% to 
50% operated working interest) in southwestern Gonzales County, Texas, beginning
in the fourth quarter of 2016.</p>

<td valign="top" style="width:3.62%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.62%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-
size:9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:9pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(3)</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-size:9pt;">See &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP 
Financial Measures&#8221; section below.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:2.47%;text-indent:-
2.47%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Rig Idle and Termination Expense</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">In the second quarter of
2016, the Company recognized a non-recurring expense of $3.8 million associated 
with the termination of a drilling rig contract that was entered into in mid-
2014 and utilized in our Eagle Ford operations from April 2015 through January 
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company temporarily idled the rig in January 2016, and 
subsequently, the Company and its rig contractor agreed to terminate the 
contract.  The total financial obligation was $5.1 million, of which $1.3 
million was recognized in the first quarter while the rig was temporarily idled 
and $3.8 million was recognized in the second quarter of 2016.  To fulfil this 
obligation, the Company issued the rig contractor a $5.1 million unsecured 
promissory note.&nbsp;&nbsp;The note amortizes over a 3-year period concluding 
in July 2019 with no pre-payment penalty.&nbsp;&nbsp;The note has an interest 
rate of 8.0% for the first 12 months, 10.0% for the second 12 months, and 12.0%
for the last 12 months.  As of June 30, 2016, $1.6 million was recorded as a 
current liability and $3.5 million was recorded as a long-term liability.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Hedging Update</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a 
name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU3"></a>During the second quarter of 2016, 
the Company entered into additional hedge transactions associated with its oil 
and natural gas production for the remainder of 2016, 2017, and 
2018.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has now hedged for the second half of 2016 
approximately 2,010 Boepd, or 44%, of the mid-point of its </p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">2016 production guidance</font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> </font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">at </font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">average</font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> oil and natural gas 
prices of $49.35/Bbl and $2.604/MMBtu, respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;Further details 
of the Company&#8217;s hedge transaction are provided in its </font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">quarterly report on Form
</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">10-Q 
for the period ended June 30, 2016.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Acquisition of Lynden Energy Corp.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">As previously announced,
the Company closed its acquisition of Lynden Energy Corp. on May 18, 2016, for 
approximately $77.8 million, financed by the issuance of approximately 3.7 
million shares of Earthstone common stock and the assumption of Lynden&#8217;s 
net financial obligations.&nbsp;&nbsp;The acquisition provides the Company with 
approximately 5,900 net acres in the Midland Basin, current net production of 
1,130 Boepd, and 100 gross horizontal locations.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Guidance Reaffirmed</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:7.25%;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company reiterates 
guidance previously disclosed on June 15, 2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;This guidance is 
subject to significant and material changes, including commodity prices and 
industry conditions.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Management Comments</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a 
name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU4"></a>Frank A. Lodzinski, President and 
Chief Executive Officer of Earthstone Energy, Inc., commented, &#8220;We had a 
number of significant accomplishments in the second quarter of 
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notably, the closing of the Lynden acquisition has increased 
our production and places the Company in a premier basin that is characterized 
by numerous zones, high recoveries, and a low cost structure.&nbsp;&nbsp;We 
welcome Lynden&#8217;s stockholders to the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, we 
successfully completed the Company&#8217;s first equity offering, raising 
approximately $50.0 million from institutional investors.&nbsp;&nbsp;We 
initially used some of these proceeds to reduce indebtedness under our revolving
credit facility from $47.8 million to $10.0 million.&nbsp;&nbsp;With increased 
financial flexibility and preservation of capital demonstrated in the first half
of </p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">2016, we believe now is an opportune time 
to complete our inventory of 12 Eagle Ford wells and will likely d</font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">o so in </font><font 
style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">the third and fourth 
quarters of</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> 
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, we may drill</font><font style="font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> five to six wells in southwestern 
Gonzales</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> 
County in </font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">the 
fourth quarter of</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: 
normal;"> 2016 and </font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: 
normal;">the first quarter of</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> 2017; however, the recent decline in 
commodity prices gives us caution, and as such, we continue to judge the merits 
of resuming drilling activities.&#8221;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>

operations.&nbsp;&nbsp;Investors and analysts are invited to participate in the 
call by dialing 877-407-8035 for domestic calls or 201-689-8035 for 
international calls, in both cases asking for the Earthstone conference 
call.</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-
family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font 
style="text-decoration:underline;">About Earthstone Energy, Inc.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: 
normal;">Earthstone Energy, Inc. is a growth-oriented independent oil and gas 
exploration and production company engaged in developing and acquiring oil and 
gas reserves through an active and diversified program that includes acquiring, 
drilling and developing undeveloped leases, asset and corporate acquisitions and
exploration activities, with its current primary assets located in the Eagle 
Ford trend of south Texas, the Midland Basin of west Texas, and in the Williston
Basin of North Dakota.&nbsp;&nbsp;Earthstone is traded on NYSE MKT under the 
symbol &#8220;ESTE.&#8221;&nbsp;&nbsp;Information on Earthstone can be found at 
www.earthstoneenergy.com.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company&#8217;s corporate headquarters 
is located in The Woodlands, Texas.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>

normal;"><br>Unaudited</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Non-GAAP Financial 
Measures</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The non-GAAP financial 
measures of Adjusted Net Income and Adjusted EBITDAX, as calculated by us below,
are intended to provide readers with meaningful information that supplements our
financial statements prepared in accordance with GAAP (U.S. Generally Accepted 
Accounting Principles). These disclosures may not be comparable to similarly 
titled measures used by other companies. Further, these non-GAAP measures should
only be considered in conjunction with financial statements and disclosures 
prepared in accordance with GAAP and should not be considered in isolation or as
a substitute for GAAP measures, such as net income or loss, operating income or 
loss, or any other GAAP measure of financial position or results of 
operations.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">I. Adjusted Net Income (Loss)</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Adjusted net income (loss) is a non-GAAP 
financial measure we use to evaluate performance, prior to non-cash gains and 
losses and non-recurring items after applying adjusted income tax 
expense.&nbsp;&nbsp;Non-cash gains and losses may include, when applicable, 
accretion, impairment expense, unrealized gains and losses on derivative 
contracts, non-cash stock compensation expense, and items that management 
considers non-recurring.  We believe adjusted net income helps investors compare
our results with other oil and natural gas companies.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The following presents a
reconciliation of income (loss) before income taxes to adjusted net income 
(loss):</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">II. Adjusted EBITDAX</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a 
name="_MON_1373442145"></a><a name="_MON_1373442158"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373442197"></a><a name="_MON_1373442465"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373442623"></a><a name="_MON_1373443675"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373461571"></a><a name="_MON_1373461597"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373461625"></a><a name="_MON_1373461652"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373461685"></a><a name="_MON_1373461723"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373461750"></a><a name="_MON_1373694593"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373712831"></a><a name="_MON_1373778887"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373789682"></a><a name="_MON_1373974507"></a><a 
name="_MON_1381146547"></a><a name="_MON_1381146786"></a><a 
name="_MON_1381153065"></a><a name="_MON_1381153086"></a><a 
name="_MON_1381556153"></a><a name="_MON_1381556191"></a><a 
name="_MON_1381575702"></a><a name="_MON_1381747850"></a><a 
name="_MON_1381832766"></a><a name="_MON_1381917093"></a><a 
name="_MON_1382160646"></a><a name="_MON_1390645189"></a><a 
name="_MON_1390915202"></a><a name="_MON_1390915216"></a><a 
name="_MON_1390915277"></a><a name="_MON_1390915298"></a><a 
name="_MON_1390915320"></a><a name="_MON_1390915361"></a><a 
name="_MON_1390915371"></a><a name="_MON_1390915468"></a><a 
name="_MON_1390991165"></a><a name="_MON_1392458738"></a><a 
name="_MON_1392731585"></a><a name="_MON_1392731604"></a><a 
name="_MON_1392793939"></a><a name="_MON_1373441960"></a><a 
name="_MON_1373442064"></a><a 
name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU10"></a>Adjusted EBITDAX is used as a 
supplemental financial measure by our management and by external users of our 
financial statements, such as investors, commercial banks and others, to assess 
our operating performance compared to that of other companies in our industry, 
without regard to financing methods, capital structure or historical costs 
basis.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is also used to assess our ability to </p>
<p style="margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">incur and service debt and fund capital 
expenditures.&nbsp;&nbsp;We define </font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-
family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;</font><font style="font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Adjus</font><font style="font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ted EBITDAX&#8221; as net income (loss) 
plus</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">, 
when applicable,</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: 
normal;"> (gain) loss on sale of assets; accretion; </font><font 
style="color:#000000;">impairment expense;</font><font style="font-
size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-
transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> d</font><font 
style="color:#000000;">epletion, depreciation, and amortization</font><font 
style="color:#000000;">; exploration expense;</font><font 
style="color:#000000;"> idle </font><font style="color:#000000;">rig 
</font><font style="color:#000000;">expense;</font><font style="color:#000000;">
interest expense;</font><font style="color:#000000;"> interest income; 
</font><font style="color:#000000;">unrealized (gain) loss on derivatives; 
</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">non-
cash stock compensation expense;</font><font style="color:#000000;"> 
</font><font style="color:#000000;">and income tax expense (benefit).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-
weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Our 
Adjusted EBITDAX should not be considered an alternative to net income (loss), 
operating income (loss), cash flow provided by (used in) operating activities or
any other measure of financial performance or liquidity presented in accordance 
with GAAP.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Adjusted EBITDAX may not be comparable to similarly 
titled measures of another company because all companies may not calculate 
Adjusted EBITDAX in the same manner.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-

style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The following table 
provides a reconciliation of net income (loss) to Adjusted EBITDAX for the 
periods indicated:</p>
